 $checkbox.prettyCheckable({color:"subscribe"});$('.js-move-cursor-on-focus').each(function(){var input=$(this),placeholder=input.mask('option','placeholder'),firstPlaceholderMatch;$(this).on('click',function(){var nextAvailablePosition=input.val().indexOf(placeholder,0),notFull=nextAvailablePosition!==-1,currentCaretPosition=input[0].selectionStart;if(typeof firstPlaceholderMatch=='undefined'){firstPlaceholderMatch=input.val().indexOf(placeholder,0);}
 if(notFull){if((currentCaretPosition>nextAvailablePosition)||(currentCaretPosition<firstPlaceholderMatch)){input[0].setSelectionRange(nextAvailablePosition,nextAvailablePosition);}}
 else if(currentCaretPosition<firstPlaceholderMatch){input[0].setSelectionRange(firstPlaceholderMatch,firstPlaceholderMatch);}});});popover=$('[data-toggle="popover"]').popover({trigger:'manual',template:'<div class="popover popover--no-wrap popover--validation popover--subscribe" role="tooltip">'+'<div class="arrow"></div>'+'<h3 class="popover-title"></h3>'+'<div class="popover-content"></div>'+'</div>'});}
 $(document).ready(function(){initOrderForm();});function SendClick(element){isPost=true;ClickOrer();Page_ClientValidate("Send");if(Page_IsValid){var formId=element.getAttribute("data-form-id");if(!formId)formId=TRACKID.SideFormIndividualRequestSend;CommonTrackClick(formId);return PreSendOrder('preSend','Send');}
 return false;}
 function ValidateQuickName(source,arguments){$(source).removeAttr("style");var target=$("input[key='quickName']");if((target.val()==''||target.val()=='Имя*:')&&isPost){arguments.IsValid=false;target.popover('show');$(source).html('');}else{$(source).html('');arguments.IsValid=true;target.popover('hide');}}
 function ValidateQuickPhone(source,arguments){var message='';var target=$("input[key='quickPhone']");if((target.val()==''||target.val()=='Телефон*:')&&isPost){target.popover('show');isPost=false;arguments.IsValid=false;}else{if(target.val()!='Телефон*:'){var expr=/\+38\(\d{3}\)\s{1}\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{2}/i;var isValid=expr.test(target.val());if(!isValid){target.popover('show');isPost=false;arguments.IsValid=false;}else{target.popover('hide');}}}
 $(source).html(message);$(source).removeAttr("style");}
 function ValidateQuickEmail(source,arguments){var message='';var target=$("input[key='quickEmail']");if(target.val()!=''&&target.val()!='E-mail:'){var re=/^(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;var isValid=re.test(target.val());if(!isValid){target.popover('show');isPost=false;arguments.IsValid=false;}else{target.popover('hide');}}
 $(source).html(message);$(source).removeAttr("style");}
